BIB                 15         65                                 2213600100002 
TITLE       Measurement and analysis of double differential       2213600100003 
            neutron emission cross sections at En = 14.1 MeV for  2213600100004 
            93Nb and 181Ta                                        2213600100005 
AUTHOR     (A.Takahashi, Y.Sasaki, H.Sugimoto)                    2213600100006 
INSTITUTE  (2JPNOSA)                                              2213600100007 
REFERENCE  (R,OKTAV-A-92-01,1992)                                 2213600100008 
            Tables (ADX,SIG,EDX,DDX) and figs (ADX,EDX,DDX) given 2213600100009 
           (R,INDC(JPN)-118,1989)                                 2213600100010 
            Slightly different tabulated ADX and EDX given        2213600100011 
REL-REF    (M,,E.Ichimura+,R,OKTAV-A-87-02,1987)                  2213600100012 
            Description of  22136001 the correction code MUSCC3   2213600100013 
FACILITY   (CCW,2JPNOSA) Intense 14 MeV neutron source OKTAVIAN   2213600100014 
INC-SOURCE (D-T) Pulsed beam with 2 ns pulse width and 1 MHz      2213600100015 
            repetition rate.                                      2213600100016 
SAMPLE     .Cylindrical niobium or tantalum metal samples with 3  2213600100017 
            cm diameter by 7 cm long. The samples were positioned 2213600100018 
            at a distance of 17 cm from the tritium target and at 2213600100019 
            right angle with respect to the deuteron beam line,   2213600100020 
            with the symmetry axis parallel to the beam line. The 2213600100021 
            scattering angle could be varied by rotating the      2213600100022 
            samples around the target along the 17 cm radius arc. 2213600100023 
            In this way measurements were performed for 16 angles 2213600100024 
            in the range 15 - 160 degrees.                        2213600100025 
           .The background was measured without sample.           2213600100026 
METHOD     (TOF) The total energy resolution was +/- 0.2 MeV.     2213600100027 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) NE-213 liquid scintillator of 25.4 cm diameter  2213600100028 
            by 10 cm thick, located at an angle of 85 degrees with2213600100029 
            respect to the deuteron beam line and at a distance of2213600100030 
            8.3 m from the tritium target. Pulse shape discrimina-2213600100031 
            tion was employed to separate neutrons and gamma-rays.2213600100032 
            the tof analysis was done for the energy range 0.5 -  2213600100033 
            14 MeV.                                               2213600100034 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA)                                 2213600100035 
            Scattering from hydrogen at an angle of 25 degrees    2213600100036 
            was used for absolute determination of the cross      2213600100037 
            section scale.                                        2213600100038 
CORRECTION  Corrections are made for                              2213600100039 
             - multiple scattering;                               2213600100040 
             - attenuation;                                       2213600100041 
             - neutron source contamination.                      2213600100042 
           !  with the help of MUSCC3 code, see REL-REF,          2213600100043 
            based on JENDL-3. In case that JENDL-3 would produce  2213600100044 
            double differential neutron emission spectrum in      2213600100045 
            drastic disagreement with the measured one, the       2213600100046 
            correction can be skipped and the adoption of raw,    2213600100047 
            i.e. experimental, data is recommended by authors.    2213600100048 
           .This correction amounted to about 10%, except for     2213600100049 
            backward elastic scattering where it could be         2213600100050 
            up to 30%.                                            2213600100051 
COMMENT    .Correction factor are calculated using evaluated data,2213600100052 
            however, they are still primitive. Calculation of cor-2213600100053 
            rection factors should be carried out again after new 2213600100054 
            version of evaluation would be published.*By authors* 2213600100055 
ERR-ANALYS .Errors defined in proper SUBENTs                      2213600100056
